Part One <%y^ 1 Sources of Archetypal Psychology Archetypal psychology, first named as such by Hillman (1970b), had from its beginning the intention of moving beyond clinical inquiry within the consulting room of psychotherapy by situating itself within the culture of Western imagination. It is a psychology deliberately affiliated with the arts, culture, and the history of ideas, arising as they do from the imagination. The term "archetypal," in contrast to "analytical" which is the usual appellation for Jung's psychol- ogy, was preferred not only because it reflected "the deep- ened theory of Jung's later work which attempts to solve psychological problems beyond scientific models" (Hillman 1970b); it was preferred more importantly because "archetypal" belongs to all culture, all forms of human activity, and not only to professional practitioners of modern therapeutics. By traditional definition, archetypes are the primary forms that govern the psyche. But they cannot be contained only by the psyche, since they manifest as well in physical, social, linguistic, aesthetic, and spiritual modes. Thus, arche- typal psychology's first links are with culture tion rather than with medical and imagina- and empirical psychologies, which tend to confine psychology to the positivistic manifestations of the nineteenth-century condition of the soul. Sources of Archetypal Psychology Archetypal psychology can be seen as a cultural movement part of whose task is the re-visioning of psychology, psychopathology, and psychotherapy in terms of the Western cultural imagination. In an early review of the field and an examination of its main thrusts, Goldenberg (1975) regards archetypal psychology as a "third generation" derivative of the Jungian school in which Jung is recognized as the source but not as the doctrine. Two themes of its directions which she singles out— the emphasis upon psychopathology and the radical relativiza- and desubstantiation of the ego — will be discussed tion below. It is without doubt that the first immediate father of arche- typal psychology is Carl Gustav Jung, the Swiss psychologist (1875-1961). Hillman,Lopez-Pedraza, Berry, Kugler,M. Stein, Guggenbiihl, Garufi, Grinnell, and many others of the authors referred to below were trained as Jungian analysts. (However, a significant number of other authors mentioned Durand, Watkins, Sardello— did not receive this specific Jungian formation and contribute to archetypal psychology from phenomenology, literature, poetry, philosophy, religious studies, etc.) From Jung comes the idea that the basic and universal structures of the psyche, the formal patterns of its relational modes, are archetypal patterns. These are like psychic organs, congenitally given —e.g., Miller, Casey, with the psyche itself (yet not necessarily genetically inherited), even if somewhat modified by historical and geograph- These patterns or archai appear in the arts, religions, dreams, and social customs of all peoples, and they manifest spontaneously in mental disorders. For Jung, they are anthropological and cultural, and also spiritual in that they transcend the empirical world of time and place and, in fact, are in themselves not phenomenal. Archetypal psycholical factors. Sources of Archetypal Psychology ogy, in distinction to Jungian, considers the archetypal to be always phenomenal (Avens 1980), thus avoiding the Kantian idealism implied in Jung (de Voogd 1977). The primary, and irreducible, language of these archetypal patterns is the metaphorical discourse of myths. These can therefore be understood as the most fundamental patterns of human existence. To study human nature at its most basic one must turn to culture (mythology, religion, art, architecture, epic, drama, ritual) where these patterns are portrayed. The full implication of this move away from biochemical, socio-historical, and personal-behavioristic bases for human nature and toward the imaginative has been articulated by Hillman as "the poetic basis of mind" (q.v.). Support for the archetypal and psychological significance of myth, besides the work of Jung, comes from Ernst Cassirer, Karl Kerenyi, Erich Neumann, Heinrich Zimmer, Gilbert Durand, Joseph Campbell, and David Miller. The second immediate father of archetypal psychology is Henry Corbin (1903-1978), the French scholar, philosopher, and mystic, principally known for his interpretation of Islamic thought. From Corbin (1971-73) comes the idea that the mundus archetypalis ('alam al-mithdl) is also the mundus imlevel, aginalis. It is a distinct field of imaginal realities requiring methods and perceptual faculties different from the spiritual world beyond it or the empirical world of usual sense perception and naive formulation. The mundus imaginalis offers an ontological mode of locating the archetypes of the psyche, as the fundamental structures of the imagination or as fun- damentally imaginative phenomena that are transcendent to the world of sense in their value if not their appearance. Their value lies in their theophanic nature and in their virtually or potentiality which is always ontologically more than actuality and its limits. (As phenomena they must ap- Sources of Archetypal Psychology pear, though this appearance is to the imagination or in the imagination.) The mundus imaginalis provides for archetypes a valuative and cosmic grounding, when this is needed» dif- ferent from such bases as: biological instinct, eternal forms, numbers, linguistic and social transmission, biochemical reactions, genetic coding, etc. But more important than the ontological placing of archetypal realities is the double move of Corbin: (a) that the fun- damental nature of the archetype is accessible to imagination first and first presents itself as image, so that (b) the entire procedure of archetypal psychology as a method is imaginative. Its exposition must be rhetorical and poetic, its reasoning not logical, and its therapeutic aim neither social adaptation nor personalistic individualizing but rather a work in service of restoration of the patient to imaginal realities. The aim of therapy (q.v.) is the development of a sense of soul, the middle ground of psychic realities, and the method of therapy is the cultivation of imagination. In extending the tradition of Jung and Corbin forward, archetypal psychology has had to go back to their predecessors, particularly the Neoplatonic tradition via Vico and the Renaissance (Ficino), through Proclus and Plotinus, to Plato {Phaedo, Phaedrus, Meno, Symposium, Timaeus), and most anciently to Heraclitus. (Corbin's works on Avicenna, Ibn' Arabi, and Sohrawardi belong also in this tradition as does the work of Kathleen Raine on William Blake [1758-1835] and on Thomas Taylor, the English translator of the main writings of Plato and the Neoplatonists.) The elaboration of this tradition by Hillman in Eranos lectures and in articles (1973a), by Miller in seminars at Syracuse University, by Lopez-Pedraza at the University of Caracas, and by Moore's (1982) and Boer's (1980) work on Ficino gives a different cast to archetypal psychology Sources of Archetypal Psychology when compared with Jung's. There the background is more strongly German (Nietzsche, Schopenhauer, Carus, von Hartmann, Kant, Goethe, Eckhart, and Bohme), Christian, psychiatric, and Eastern. Archetypal psychology situates itself more comfortably south (q.v.) of the Alps. Especially— this Neoplatonic tradition is thoroughly Western even if it is not empirical in method, rationalist in conception, or otherworldly spiritual in appeal. This tradition holds to the notion of soul as a first principle, placing this soul as a tertium between the perspectives of body (matter, nature, empirics) and of mind (spirit, logic, idea). Soul as tertium, the perspective between others and from which others may be viewed, has been described as Hermetic con(i ammo," (Jung [1921] CW 6, §66, 77), as the position of the mundus imaginalis by Corbin, and by Neoplatonic writers on the intermediaries or figures of the metaxy. Body, soul, spirit: this tripartite anthropology further separates archetypal psychology from the usual Western dualistic division, whose history goes back sciousness (Lopez-Pedraza 1977), as esse in before Descartes to at least the ninth century (869: Eighth General Council mediaeval at ascension Constantinople), occurring also in the of Averroes's Aristotelianism over Avicenna's Platonism. Consequences of this dualistic division are still being felt in that the psyche has become indistinguishable from bodily life, on the one hand, or from the life of the spirit on the other. In the dualistic tradition, psyche never had its own logos. There could be no true psyfirst methodologically consistent attempt to chology. A articulate one in a philosophical style belongs also within the perimeters of archetypal psychology (Christou 1963). —...

 GENERATORS' COURSE RA URU HU SEDONA ARIZONA FEBRUARY 2003 GENERATORS: TRULY HOLY THROUGH SURRENDER Over the last five and a half weeks I have been traveling extensively doing what is in fact my last tour. And one of the main emphases of this tour is to make sure particularly that Generators get the message. I've spent most of my teaching career focused almost exclusively on Generators and the potential of being able to awaken Generators. There's nothing more special on this planet than Generators; and what I mean by that is that out of the Sacral Center, and only Generators have a defined Sacral Center, that out of the Sacral Center what you get is the generation of life itself, literally. And it means that whatever we consider to be the life process, whatever we consider to be the quality and the reality of life on this Earth, that life on this Earth is created by Generators. It is their work. You know, this is the fundamental difference between Generators and all other types, is that all other types are not born to work - they are born to find life. It's a great joke by the way, you know, the difference between finding a life and getting a job, and if you're a Sacral being, you come into the world to find the right work. And it's only once you've found the right work that you get your life. Everything about being a Generator is the fact that the Generator is a prime motor, and to really understand the nature of that prime motor. It's not metamorphic; it's simply a motor. It's very, very powerful. It's the kind of motor that doesn't give up, that doesn't stop, and that keeps on going; that the Generator is designed to operate to the point of exhaustion every day, every day. The essence of being a Generator is that if you're using your energy properly you reach a point of exhaustion each day that's perfect for you. That's perfect. This is their process. It is their process. The gods on the other end say, "Okay, you know, basically it's easy for them, but let's make it as difficult as possible." It's mechanically incredibly easy. It's driven me crazy over the years. I live in a Generator-dominated world. I live in this incredible world of Generator frustration, and my frustration, that is my amplified frustration with Generators! Most of the time, I want to hit them! [laughter] Really, "Whack!" You know? Just hit them, "Hey, why don't you get it, it's so simple!" When I first started, truly, when I first started, one of the main motivations I had other than I saw...

### I Ching Philosophy

**Hebrew to GeneKeys Codon Rings PDF 1**

*Topics: archetypes, individuation, alchemy, collective_unconscious, symbols, transformation, soul, mythology, healing, systemic, energy, i_ching*

Hebrew Letters to Gene Keys Codon Rings Created by Karen (Kat) Benson The correlations of Hebrew Letters to Amino Acids is based on the work of Steve Krakowski. Sources for information and inspiration came from the following sources: Glorian Publishing Soul Contract Reading system Enneagram Rawn Clark 32 Paths if Wisdom Gene Keys I Ching translation Anthony & Moog The Energy of Hebrew Letters Rav Berg The 7 Rays, Dr. J. David Stone Kabbalist Samuel Avital’s work Too many other unknown sources And, my own intuitive creative inspirations! This work is not sanctioned by Richard Rudd or the Gene Keys community 1 – ‫ א‬Aleph: Unity and Strength, Power, Perfection The ‘1’ symbolizes the Great wind that hovers over the waters of creation; the firmament that separates the watery physical realm from the Supernal Realm, Plan of God, the great mind, the breath of divinity that gives all life, From Unity to multiplicity, where the 3 Great forces emerge, creating something from nothing, the One that cannot be divided, cannot be spoken about, present everywhere, timeless, spaceless, Perfection. 1st Ray of creation = Divine Will, Power, Strength =============================================================== Major Arcana: Element: The Fool Air Amino Acid: Affected Physiologies: None (Terminator Codon) Thyroid, Throat Codon Ring: Ring of Trials (stuck in past, illusion of individuality, distractions) Gene Keys/Hex: 33, 56 (Heaven/Mountain, Fire/Mountain) Victim of: Fear: Desire: Seeking: False Belief: You need to hear: Wound/Passion: Need to be perfect & Memories Being bad, corrupt, evil, defective…not good/godly enough To have integrity, aligned with “the good”, the Sacred, to be virtuous. Perfection It’s not okay to make mistakes. You are good Repression/Anger/Resentment =============================================================== Shadow: (Forgetting, Distractions), Striving, opinionated, high minded, “should and musts”, imposing order, ambition, willfulness, hardness, arrogance, seeking power, strongly held views, making others wrong to feel right, fault-finding, feel imperfect, fussy, angry, resentful, disapproving, inflexible, self-righteous, denouncing, unforgiving feeling corrupt or possessed, tormented, cruel, attacking, self-harming, full of hate and self-hate. Gifts:(Mindfulness, Revelation, Enrichment, Intoxication), Directed purpose, direct channel to and for Divine Mind, dynamic power, spiritual and physical strength, detachment, courage, truthful, responsible, principled, ethical, proactive, teach by example, good humored, tolerant, seek greater good, okay with uncertainty, have integrity, discerning warm-hearted, noble, pure, “Right Action”, feel the goodness of life, accepting and wise. Karma/Samskaras: Situations involving power issues, manipulation or abuse to or from others, particularly from the masculine, issues around any patriarchal or rule based system (government, religion, parents), denying the masculine or power within oneself. Cosmic Principle: Perfect Consciousness - Stillness is your Highest Potential, Growth comes from fire, the destruction of one thing into another. The ‘1’ aka The One is not an active force, It just is, passive. It is always there, It is everywhere and in every thing. It is your Silent Partner. This silence is perfection. It is The One who watches the mind, It reveals, It intoxicates, It holds the Plan of the Primordial. ‘1’ represents the final of 3 trials that Kundalini must pass thru, at the throat, in order for Her to reach upper upper process/crown, which eventually leads to non-dual perception or Oneness. The trails consist of Letting go of all thoughts that denigrate Life, yourself and animal nature. (“Life is suffering, I’m not good enough, spiritual enough, higher self better than personality, release all guilt and doubt) Time to recognize your Inner Truth, no to blaming life or others, let go of techniques/practices particularly in meditation they are for the mind block your inner knowing, your own inner meditation, become the Wanderer, one who follows his inner truth, not a person on the spiritual journey, who follows what is laid out by another, let go of the spiritual image of “good person or one seeking “perfection”, and let go at looking at life as something to be transcended. =============================================================== 2 – ‫ ב‬Beth Double Number: Resiliency: Trial & Error – Foolishness to Wisdom The ‘2’ is the vehicle for Aleph-1 or Divine Will it is our feelings, She is the Cosmic Mother representing duality, She is Consciousness, our feeling body., creative force, the Receiver, the body, the vessel of the Souls, ’2’ is called the House of God, enter this house through the heart. Only letter capable of washing away the illusion and providing internal/eternal connection to the Absolute. 2nd Ray of Love, Wisdom, Illumination =============================================================== Major Arcana: Planet/Zodiac: The Magus/Magician Mercury Codon Ring: Ring of Union Amino Acids: Affected Physiologies: Valine Neocortex, Diaphragm, Sacral Plexus Gene Keys/Hex: 4, 7, 29, 59 (Mountain/Water, Earth/Water, Water/Water, Wind/Water) Victim of: Fear: Desire: Seeking: False Belief: You need to hear: Wound/Passion: Need for answers, Jealousy, Commitments, Relationships Being unloved, unlovable, unworthy of love, not having love. To be loved, to be one with Love, to be the source of Love. Closeness It’s not okay to have your own needs You are wanted Denial, Pride, Flattery, Ingratiation =============================================================== Shadow:(Intolerance, Division, Half-Heartedness, Dishonesty) Demonstrative, seeking relationships, consumed with relationships, intrusive, possessive, ulterior motives, gossiping, overbearing, over-sensitivity/failure. self-important ‘saint’, effusive friend, manipulative, guilt instilling, histrionic, entitled, ruining relationships, demanding repayment, feeling victimized, psychosomatic, parasitic, deeply bitter, exploding rage. Gifts: (Understanding/Forgiveness, Guidance/Virtue, Commitment/Devotion, Intimacy/ Transparency)Supportive, appreciative, nurturing, helpful, giving, caring, emotionally aware, compassionate, responsive, loving, empathetic, full of grace, contemplative, radiant, unselfish, joyous, altruist, unconditional love. Karma/Samskaras: Emotionally charged situations, especially within relationships, seeking love, need to be loved, needing relationships, needing to be source of love, emotional decisions, perceiving failure. Cosmic Principle: Overflowing Consciousness - The Creator of all that is. The emanation of the most ethereal essences and powers, as well as the densest of light. Creator of Duality, Subject Object consciousness. Must develop Right Relationship with Life, by bringing the ‘1’, stillness into the heart, into the unconscious and witness w/o comment or reaction all that is occurring. Once must understand form and the relative world, three is divine consequence behind everything. Cosmic mother represents duality "For any exaltation there must be a humiliation. In order to ascend you must first descend." Freedom from conflict/duality only achieved thru body, feeling/sensing consciousness not emotions - feel it to heal it. You are the conflict, the duality. Most important relationship is w/cosmos and your True Self. Trust your inner feeling/senses not your emotions. Never see others as “culprits/evil’, even when they are the aggressor as this creates fates for both and assassinates their True Nature. Don’t fear death there is no “abyss” (you are the abyss), all primal fears arise in mind, connect with body for Truth. With Sincerity ask for help and your heart will have success. It is your fears that create ‘dark beings’, call on Helpers NEVER throw away true self by entering into relationship to get something, ask your Helpers instead, Dissolve your dependence on collective ego, including groups of ‘like minded’, who think as “we/family, etc, we are your tribe”, this is a trap. Fears and self-doubt keep you attached to group/collective. =============================================================== 3– ‫ ג‬Gimel: Master Double Number: Poverty to Wealth Expression/Activity The ‘3’ is ‘the one who has started walking’ 3rd leg of the Trinity – Father, Mother, Child - dynamic balancing force between 1 & 2, ’3’ represents Law of Giving thru Intelligent Expression, Mercy & Doer of good deeds. Also the movement between opposites/complementary forces - motion and change. Represents reward and punishment, law of judgment, in alignment, in receipt of goodness or not. 3 is inseparable from 4. 3rd Ray of Intelligent Activity =============================================================== Major Arcana: Planet/Zodiac: The High Priestess Luna/Moon Amino Acids: Affected Physiologies: Isoleucine Body Hair, Colon, Pineal Gland Codon Ring: Gene Keys/Hex: Ring of Gaia (looking outside oneself for guidance (god) co-dependence, reactive rigid thinking and constantly wanting to know why – psychosis) 19, 60, 61 (Earth/Lake, Water/Lake, Wind/Lake) Victim of: Fear: Desire: Seeking: False Belief: You need to hear: Wound/Passion: Over-Sensitivity, Structures, Obsessive Mind Not having value, being worthless, or deficient in value. To feel valuable and worthwhile In search of validation It’s not okay to have your own feelings and expression. You are loved for yourself Vanity, Deceit, Shame =============================================================== Shadow:(Co-Dependence, Limitations, Doubt, Over-Sensitivity, Structures, Obsessive Mind) Overriding concern with how one presents themselves, how they look and what impact they have on others. Chameleons, creating a favorable impression, reading others, cool, white lies, showing off, narcism, vain, comparing, competitive, goal/ achievement oriented, needing constant attention, too much talking/never speaks up, detached from heart, unable to connect with or express true feelings, stealing backstabbing, affectless, hiding pain and madness, sadistic, vengeful, remorseless. Gifts: (Sensitivity, Realism, Inquiry, Sacrifice, Justice, Sanctity) 3 is the energy of doing, Competent, always evolving, adaptable, versatile, role-model, great motivational speakers/coaches, charming, good communicators, industrious, self-assured, feeling worthwhile/valuable, heart-centered, modest, self-accepting, truthful, sincere, inspiring, esteemed, authentic and Inner-Directed. Great performers, teachers, counselors, motivational speakers. Karma/Samskaras: Situations where your voice/feelings were not valued or heard, no voice, being under-valued or over-valued - pushed to achieve/win/compete, may have sexual intimacy issues, deep seated need to be validated/ confirmed, needing attention, talk too much or very shy hiding from world, not speaking/wall flower, image and status conscious, not telling truth about true feelings, no access to feelings, feeling totally ashamed of who you are. Cosmic Principle: Transparent Consciousness - 3rd aspect of 3 great forces 3=Neutrality, being in a state of openness, leads to clear and un-obstructive connection to Divine Will, creation, expression. Neutrality also in regards to unconscious reactions/emotions. 3 & 4 inseparable-3=to be open in order give/to express, 4= receiving and manifesting. 3=change/motion and harmony - no thing acts on its own, there is no individual doer, just one Being, therefore harmony/interdependency always exists. Say No to the spell “I have to do it all alone/all by myself, there is not help,. Release images of being “the achiever, the doer ”. Always call upon the Helpers for everything. When we do that it is for both’s evolution. Always give thanks and never claim success as your own When Helpers are not involved, limits or fates are placed on you to bring you back to humility and harmony. Must also have interdependency with our physical senses = commonsense, which will show you truth of situation by inner yes/no - does it smell right, feel right, taste right. When we rely on our inner senses then we are protected and defended by cosmos. Once you know truth, do not try to convince others as this sends a signal/spell that they are incapable of connecting with their own inner sense of truth - this has damaging affects. =============================================================== 4 – ‫ ד‬Dalet: Poverty transforms into Trust & Sharing - Barren to Fruitful Related to Greek Delta, 2 deltas create Star of David/MerKaBa/Light Body 4 & 3 represent the merging of the formless and form. Also, the doorway through which things change, doorway to Eden-Prosperity(you are the doorway), thru Knowledge of the TrueSelf. Represents law of receiving, but on its own is “poor”, needs 3-law of giving and interdependency of the cosmos to become fully prosperous and manifest. Represents 4 elements of creation - 4 chemicals/bases of DNA, structures and form. Also, represent the state of o Selflessness and Humility to pass through doorway, 4 must be in state of Receiving, Rich Man 4th Ray- Harmony thru Conflict =============================================================== Major Arcana: Planet/Zodiac: The Empress Venus Amino Acids: Affected Physiologies: Proline (non polar/charged/hydrophobic) Solar Plexus, Cranial and Dorsal Ganglia Codon Ring: Gene Keys/Hex: Ring of Divinity 22, 36, 37, 63, (Mountain/Fire, Earth/Fire, Wind/Fire, Water/Fire) Victim of: Fear: Desire: Seeking: False Belief: You need to hear: Wound/Passion: Ungracious behavior, vulnerability, gender identity and doubt Not having any personal significance, unique identity. To discover my true self/my significance, my gifts, to be myself. Identity (special or different Identity) It’s not okay to be myself, there must be something wrong with me.
